Domestic News

Central Party Headquarters and National Government's Memorial Week 57

At 9:00 AM on the 29th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 79th Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week in the Grand Auditorium. Present were Central Committee members Wu Jingheng, Dai Chuanxian, Chen Guofu, Liu Luyin, Chen Lifu, Cheng Tianfang, etc., as well as staff from various departments and committees and guests, totaling about 500 to 600 people. Dai Chuanxian chaired the meeting. After the ceremony, Wu Jingheng gave a report, stating in summary that the central troops are making progress on the front lines every day, which is encouraging from a military perspective. Yan Xishan, under the guise of courteous concessions, is attempting to achieve his ambition of seizing political power, assuming that he can obtain it without effort. However, those who comply survive while those who resist perish, and it is difficult to escape the universal rule. He is only taking the path of self-destruction. Feng Yuxiang, unable to achieve much on his own, is finding it difficult to collude with evildoers, causing his subordinates to superficially praise peace in order to ease the situation. Those in the know all understand that his ambition has not died. Judging from the current situation, he is still relying on the Niangziguan and Tongguan passes, hoping to preserve the remaining strength of the two divisions and revive them in the future. If this is not thoroughly resolved, there is no full guarantee of lasting peace. As for Wang Jingwei, who left Ping after being frustrated and issued a telegram advocating four matters: (1) convene a national conference, (2) reopen the Third National Congress, (3) revise the provisional constitution, and (4) jointly eliminate the Communist Party, the second reason is insufficient, and there is obviously another purpose. The fourth item is a tool for deceiving the people and has no value for discussion. Now, regarding the first and third items, our party initiated the Northern Expedition in the 15th year, cleared the communists in the 16th year, and completed the sound government in the 17th year. It planned to implement the reorganization conference step by step, according to the teachings of Sun Yat-sen, in order to promote unification, consolidate the foundation of the country, and give the people a way to recuperate. Yan and Feng came to Beijing and added obstacles, and the conference barely came to an end, with rebellion arising from it. Fires of war are raging, and the country is in a state of devastation. The people do not even have time to save their own lives. How can they leisurely discuss politics? As for the Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China, it has many shortcomings. Sun Yat-sen, in order to seek fundamental salvation, formulated the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction, the Strategies of National Reconstruction, and the Three Principles of the People as the basis for political tutelage, so that the general public could receive adequate training and have a deep understanding. When political tutelage is completed, a national assembly will be convened to produce a constitution and complete a democratic constitutional state. I ask, in this day and age, who can create another law to surpass the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction, the Strategies of National Reconstruction, and the Three Principles of the People, which were written by the unparalleled Sun Yat-sen? Sun Yat-sen said that knowing is difficult but doing is easy. As long as party members and the general public can understand the principles, they will not overstep the boundaries. The effectiveness of any law is rarely better than this. In this time of crisis, domestic concerns are not yet over, and foreign forces are likely to invade. It is hoped that Yan and Feng can show a little conscience, lay down their butcher knives, and heed the warning that those who are unrepentant will burn themselves. All comrades in our party and compatriots throughout the country should rise up together, follow the principles, abandon destruction and seek construction, in order to reverse the fate of disaster." The meeting adjourned after the report.

At 10:00 AM on the same day, the National Government held a Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Present were Gu Yingfen, Zhu Peide, Ma Fuxiang, Yi Peiji, Jiang Menglin, Zhang Nanxian, Qiu Ao, Liu Ruiheng, Chen Yi, Chen Shaokuan, Mu Xiangyue, Zhou Yawei, Zhang Wohua, Chen Yu, Wu Siyu, and over 200 staff members from the National Government's civil service and military affairs departments. Gu Yingfen chaired the meeting. Following the ceremony, Secretary Qian Changzhao gave a political report, as follows: "Last week, President Tan Yankai passed away, which is a great loss to the party and the country. Everyone knows his revolutionary history, his scholarship is admired by the general public, and his morality is the most unattainable. At this moment, I will list a few points: (1) Self-cultivation: He was willing to suffer losses on small matters and did not engage in unnecessary disputes. On big matters, he had a firm position and dealt with them calmly. This attitude certainly has the style of a great statesman. (2) Tolerance: His mind was like a vast ocean, all-encompassing. He absolutely did not envy those who were higher than him in position, he absolutely did not act impulsively towards those who were equal to him in position, and he absolutely did not show any arrogance towards those who were lower than him in position. In his daily life, he was kind and approachable, with an inviolable dignity. He was indeed a role model for the people. (3) Perseverance: He was always profound and diligent in his work throughout his life, and his spirit was always unremitting. Sometimes, the more difficult the environment, the more his perseverance was shown. He was worthy of being a pillar of the party and the country. (4) Integrity: He did not take a single bribe in the military and political circles for twenty or thirty years. He himself had no savings. In today's China, this alone is enough to rectify bad habits. Since President Tan's revolutionary history, scholarship, and morality are so great, and he was only fifty-two years old, not yet at an age of decline, and yet had signs of premature aging, the reason was entirely due to his devotion to the party and the country. Recently, his health has been extremely poor, and even to the point that he had shortness of breath and could not finish reading Sun Yat-sen's will during meetings or memorial weeks. We were worried about his health, and the doctors repeatedly advised him to rest. However, in recent months, the military situation on the front lines has been tense, and it is very important to be in charge in the rear. His love for the party and the country ultimately outweighed his love for his own body. He carried on with his responsibilities while ill, day and night. Now that the military situation on the front lines is about to end, he will soon be able to take a short rest, but he has passed away. From now on, we will no longer be able to hear his calm footsteps in this hall, and we will no longer be able to see his gentle appearance. How memorable and painful this is. Last Friday, the State Council resolved to issue a decree for a state funeral. At the same time, we should emulate President Tan's character and work even harder to make the revolution a success as soon as possible, in order to comfort President Tan in the afterlife. The military victory on the front lines, Lanfeng has already been recovered, and Kaifeng and Zhengzhou will be captured soon. The obstacles to peace can be removed soon, and a long period of tranquility in the country can be obtained. After the military situation ends, the most important thing, of course, is to eradicate the bandits and the communists, so that the people can live and work in peace. Now there are many places where people have been displaced and the foundations of society have been shaken due to the harassment of the bandits and the communists. The government is very concerned and will definitely take responsibility to eliminate the harm and restore social order for the people. At the same time, it will concentrate all kinds of forces on construction. One is to solve the livelihood problems for the people, the second is to increase domestic wealth, and the third is to resist foreign economic aggression. In short, this is the best opportunity to reorganize the country. I have said that the transition from a country where politics is not fully on track to one where politics is clean and bright often comes after a major upheaval. Because after a major upheaval, the government wins, its prestige is established, and as long as it makes a firm decision to do it, it will naturally be twice as effective. This time, the government will eliminate the rebels such as Yan and Feng, and it is a good opportunity to resolutely and boldly carry out the things that should be promoted and reformed in the country, and progress may be made by leaps and bounds. But there is one thing that should be taken into account, that is, there are many things that should be promoted and reformed in the country, and for all things, before deciding to promote and reform and when implementing the promotion and reform, we must have a detailed observation of the overall situation of the country, so that we can prescribe the right medicine. Otherwise, a slight deviation will lead to a great error, and danger will occur. Therefore, all preparatory work is very important, and I hope everyone will pay attention to it.

Completion of the Luokou Railway Bridge on the Jinpu Railway 58

Jinan correspondence: The Luokou Yellow River Railway Bridge, which has been actively repaired by the Jinpu Railway Engineering Department, Hu Shenghong, Chen Dawo, etc., together with the Central Railway Team, and supervised the workers in recent days, was repaired at 4:00 AM this morning. At 10:30 AM, Wei Jinglu, the captain of the Central Railway Team, accompanied by Hu Shenghong, the engineer of the Jinpu Railway, Mao Qihuan, the chief of the vehicle section, etc., took a special train of the Railway Team to Luokou for inspection, and then drove across the Yellow River Bridge northward to Dezhou to investigate whether there was any damage along the way in order to repair it. It is reported that the construction of the Yellow River Railway Bridge started on the 24th and was completed today (27th), a total of only four days from start to finish, which can be said to be fast. The iron plate of one hole in the heart of the river is still moved back to the original holes on both sides, and the iron beams and iron plates transported from Yanzhou are installed in the holes in the heart of the river. Because the materials are all original, the repair is easier. However, although the bridge has been completed and can be opened to traffic, the damaged area of the first crossbeam of the tenth hole is now being filled with stones and scaffolding, which will not be completed until the evening of the 28th. Before it is completed, only small locomotives on this route can be used to pass at a speed of five miles per hour. Other types of locomotives cannot pass. Therefore, the Railway Team's special train heading north also used the No. 69 small engine of the Jinpu Station to tow it. The Railway Bureau originally intended to order the No. 326 locomotive of the armored train to go to the bridge for a test run, but later it was temporarily abandoned because it was feared that something was wrong. Chen Dawo, the engineer of the Jinpu Railway, has already sent a telegram to Chen Weixin, the commander of the Transportation Office of the Third Route Army, and Fu Jianheng, the commander of the armored car, notifying them of the completion of the repair of the Yellow River Bridge and the restrictions on the passage of locomotives. The original telegram is as follows: "The Yellow River Bridge was completed at 4 o'clock this morning and is now open to traffic. However, the damaged area of the first crossbeam of the tenth hole is now being filled with stones and scaffolding. Before the wooden frame is set up, only smaller locomotives on this route are allowed to pass at a speed of five miles per hour. Other types of locomotives will be temporarily suspended. Please check and acknowledge. The wooden frame is expected to be completed tomorrow night." It is also heard that," (27th)

The Canton Restaurant Guild's Strike Comes to an End 59

Resulting from Repeated Petitions by the Restaurant Trade

The Provincial Government Agrees to Return the Formal Banquet Tax to the Trade for Handling

(Guangzhou Dispatch) Since opposing the use of a joint business license number for the formal banquet tax, the Guangzhou restaurant trade has been unanimously closed for twenty days. Although some have resumed business in recent days, they only sell tea, snacks, and noodles. Formal banquets, however, have consistently been suspended. The formal banquet merchants have petitioned the provincial government several times, but without success. The merchants initially requested: 1. That the authorities abolish the joint license requirement for the formal banquet tax to eliminate excessive levies; 2. If the joint license cannot be abolished, they requested that the formal banquet tax be managed by the restaurant trade itself. Later, although the Department of Finance approved the return of the formal banquet tax to the trade, it stipulated an annual payment of 800,000 yuan. This amount is almost double the current 400,000+ yuan paid by the tax merchants. Therefore, the merchants believed this demand was intentionally making things difficult for them, and the takeover remained unresolved. The restaurants remained closed as before. However, during the closure, thousands of workers employed by the restaurant trade suddenly lost their jobs and were unable to meet their basic needs, a truly pitiful situation. As a result, the restaurant workers jointly petitioned the provincial government, urging authorities to resolve the issue quickly to alleviate their suffering. On the morning of the 22nd, over a thousand workers, carrying small flags inscribed with "Please Government Support Unemployed Workers" and "Down with Formal Banquet Tax Racketeers," arrived at the provincial government. They then sent several representatives to request an audience with Provincial Chairman Chen Mingshu. They waited until about 2 PM when Chen returned to the government building. The workers nominated Liang Wensao, Lin Bao, Feng Heng, and He Zhen to meet with Chen, strongly stating that the restaurant trade usually employs several thousand workers. Due to the refusal to use joint licenses, the restaurants have closed in succession, indirectly causing thousands of workers to become unemployed. They pointed out that most workers have families of seven or eight, relying on their monthly wages for sustenance. Losing their jobs would leave their families destitute, forcing them to appeal to the government for a quick resolution to the restaurant trade issue, allowing the thousands of workers to once again rely on their jobs for sustenance. Chen, recognizing the workers were innocently affected, advised them to return and assured them the government would provide a solution the next day. After the representatives conveyed Chen's message, the workers, expecting good news in the morning, chose to camp outside the provincial government overnight to demonstrate their resolve. That evening, the workers prepared bedding and oil lamps, sleeping on the open ground in front of the provincial government. Businesses that had dealings with the restaurant trade sent cakes, tea, and water to feed the petitioners. The De Xuan Police Station dispatched officers to protect the scene until the next morning (the 23rd), maintaining good order. By 9 AM on the 23rd, Chen Mingshu had arrived at the provincial government. The 115th provincial meeting was scheduled for that day. After discussing various matters, Chen proposed a solution to the formal banquet tax issue. The outcome was that the use of joint licenses for the formal banquet tax should proceed as planned and the decision could not be reversed. The current annual payment of 417,000 yuan by the banquet tax merchant, would be returned to the restaurant trade with a new rate originally set at 800,000 yuan. In order to reach a compromise, the Department of Finance would reduce it by 200,000 yuan, and the restaurant trade would take it over with a payment of 610,000 yuan. Secretary Mei was then dispatched to convey this solution to the restaurant trade's representatives and the Chamber of Commerce. After seeking the opinion of everyone, the entire trade agreed to the government-approved annual payment of 610,000 yuan and take the formal banquet tax back to be handled by the restaurants. It was decided that representatives would be sent to the Department of Finance again today to discuss the specific details of the takeover. If there is progress, all city restaurants may resume operations in a day or two. (September 24th)

Xiamen Business Community Opposes the Reinstatement of Export Duties 60

Telegraphing the National Government's Ministry of Finance to Revoke the Order

(Xiamen Dispatch) Hou Liwei, the Xiamen Customs Commissioner, requested and obtained approval from the Ministry of Finance to reinstate the re-export duty on foreign goods transshipped to the interior and set October 1st as the implementation date. On the 4th of this month, the Xiamen Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Shantou Chamber of Commerce, inquiring whether Shantou Customs levied re-export duties. They then received a reply stating that foreign goods imported through Shantou and transshipped to the interior had historically only been taxed at the time of import in Shantou, and no further taxes were levied by the common customs when transshipping to the interior. There had been no recent changes to the tax system. After receiving the reply, the Xiamen Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of all trades in Xiamen on the 23rd to discuss the matter. They unanimously resolved to oppose the reinstatement of export duties. They also designated representatives to petition the Xiamen Customs Superintendent's Office on the 24th, urging them to forward the matter to the Ministry of Finance and revoke the order and to not implement the collection on October 1st. The Superintendent's Office agreed to forward the matter, but stated that the re-export duty was ordered by the Inspector General of Customs and the Xiamen Customs had no choice but to comply. Since businesses felt the order was difficult, they could temporarily register the taxes due pending the resolution of the case. If the Ministry of Finance agreed to abolish the duty, the payments would be waived. If the original order was maintained, the businesses would make the payments. On the 25th, the General Chamber of Commerce convened another meeting of all trades and resolved the following three items: (1) Telegraph the National Government's Ministry of Finance, urging them to instruct the authorities to prevent the implementation to safeguard commerce; (2) Unless the Ministry of Finance explicitly orders otherwise, all import and export shipments will be suspended from the deadline (food to and from the interior is exempt); (3) An anti-common customs duty on inland exports committee of Xiamen trade associations will be organized to handle all aspects of the struggle. That evening, the foreign goods import businesses telegraphed Shanghai and Hong Kong to stop shipping pending a resolution. On the 26th, the General Chamber of Commerce separately telegraphed the National Government and the Ministry of Finance, requesting the cancellation of the re-export duty. The telegram read as follows: "Respectfully to Chairman Jiang of the Nanjing National Government and Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, the Xiamen Customs Commissioner Hou Liwei is not familiar with the local situation and disregards the difficulties of the merchants, changing the common customs regulations and misrepresenting the situation to his superiors, who have approved the collection of re-export duties on goods transshipped to the interior starting October 1st. Xiamen merchants believe this move hinders commerce and stifles opportunity. All Xiamen merchants have been meeting in their respective associations to discuss the issue. They all agree that common customs duties are implemented in accordance with local conditions, and there is no uniformity across regions. Xiamen is close to Shantou and both serve as transshipment hubs. In Shantou, foreign goods are taxed by the Chaozhou Customs at the time of import, and no further taxes are levied by common customs when transshipped to the interior. Xiamen's situation is the same. If Xiamen is treated differently, merchants will inevitably choose Shantou over Xiamen to reduce tax rates. If so, the future of Xiamen's commerce is dire. We all operate under the same flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun. Why does the government favor Shantou over Xiamen? Are the Xiamen merchants responsible for something, deserving of being crushed? In recent years, Xiamen has been burdened by excessive taxes. In addition to the regular duties collected by customs on imported goods, merchants must also pay various other miscellaneous taxes, making it difficult to survive. Many choose to ship goods directly from Hong Kong and Shantou to the interior, causing commerce to decline sharply in recent years. If the common customs changes its regulations again and collects re-export duties, and the interior is plagued by bandits who disregard government orders, even if merchants pay sub-port duties in Xiamen, each region in the interior will still require them to pay local likin taxes. This is like skinning the same cow multiple times and picking the same melon multiple times. It not only violates the principles of taxation but also puts Xiamen's commerce in an impossible situation, which is not the intention of our National Government to protect commerce. Furthermore, with the implementation of the new tariff schedules imminent, common customs should be abolished. Xiamen Customs should not overturn the regulations during this brief period, as the public revenue gained is minimal and it will doom Xiamen's merchants. Based on the above facts and reasons, we have unanimously and resolutely decided to resist. We earnestly request that the authorities revoke the order to collect re-export duties on goods transshipped from Xiamen. Otherwise, merchants will be left with no choice but to collectively suspend shipments and stop imports and exports. The associations believe that the merchants see the implementation of this tax as a matter of life and death and are determined to resist it at all costs. If it is implemented, it will surely cause unrest and harm both public order and commerce. We feel it is our duty to express our concerns and dare not remain silent. We respectfully request that you, our superiors, have compassion on the merchants and instruct the Xiamen Customs Commissioner not to implement the collection of re-export duties on goods transshipped to the interior to satisfy public opinion and protect commerce. We urgently submit this plea and beg for your instructions. Respectfully, Hong Hongru, Chen Ruqing, Huang Yizhu, Chairman of the Xiamen General Chamber of Commerce. (September 26th)"

Shen Honglie Inspects the Navy in Harbin 61

Also to Reorganize Shipping Affairs

(Harbin Dispatch) Shen Honglie, Commander of the Northeast Navy, arrived in Harbin from Liaoning at 8 AM on the 21st, accompanied by Wang Shuncun, Executive Director of the Northeast Navigation Bureau. Xie Zhizhou, Commander of the River Defense Fleet, Yin Zuyin, Director of the Naval River Transportation Office, Wang Shize, Manager of the Northeast Shipping Bureau, and others welcomed him at the station. After disembarking, Shen proceeded to the Northeast Navigation Bureau. Li Siting, the marine corps commander who was once rumored to have died in the Battle of Sanjiangkou two years ago, also came with him. Shen plans to stay in Harbin for four or five days before heading to Shenyang. His mission is reportedly to inspect the Navy and to reorganize shipping affairs. At 8 AM on the 22nd, the Li Sui and Jiang Tong gunboats docked in the middle of the river at Qidaojie to await Shen's inspection. At 8:30 AM, Shen, accompanied by Fleet Commander Xie Zhizhou and others, boarded the Jiangying speedboat and first went to the Li Sui gunboat for a roll call and address, which lasted about half an hour. He then went to the Jiang Tong gunboat for an address. Afterwards, he delivered a lecture to Captain Zhang of the Li Sui and Captain Wu of the Jiang Tong. He then traveled by car to the Quanhe Barracks to inspect the sailors stationed there. He also entered the shipyard to inspect the Jiang Tai, Jiang An, and Li Jie gunboats under repair. He returned to the Navigation Bureau at about 1 PM. In the afternoon, he crossed the river to inspect the Jiangbei Shipyard and the Merchant Marine School. The Northeast United Navigation Bureau had already prepared proposals and plans to convene a general meeting of shipping merchants within two or three days to discuss the bureau's strategies and unresolved issues. It is reported that the Marine Corps may be transferred as a result of Shen's visit. (September 22nd)

Wuhu Quick Dispatch 62

At 9 AM today, the party, government, military, schools, and mass organizations held a conference to condemn the communists at the YMCA. Five to six hundred people attended, and many speakers from various sectors gave speeches. The meeting adjourned at 11 AM. Approximately three hundred bandits suddenly appeared at Bijiaqiao in Xuancheng County a few days ago. They posted slogans, kidnapped people, and demanded ransoms. Fortunately, the 3rd Battalion Commander Feng Jinghai of the Garrison Regiment under the 6th District Bandit Suppression Headquarters, who was dispatched from Wuhu to Guangde to suppress bandits, passed through the area and surrounded the bandits. The bandits were quickly routed, with some fleeing towards Guangde. The farmers of Wanchun Township and other areas in Wuhu jointly resisted rent. The county government, acting on orders from the provincial government, has arrested Cui Qifa, who instigated the resistance. However, it has been found that farmers are still marching in groups, coercing others to resist rent. A team was dispatched to the countryside again today to investigate and make arrests. The 6th District Bandit Suppression Headquarters executed a captured bandit named Wang Gongkai at the Shisandaomen at 1 PM today. (September 28th)

Local Dispatch: Songjiang 63

Minister Niu's Brief Visit to Songjiang: Niu Yongjian, Minister of Interior of the National Government, arrived in Songjiang from Shanghai by an early train at about 9 AM this morning (the 29th). Traveling inconspicuously, he went directly to the county government. He was greeted by County Magistrate Jin just as the weekly memorial service was ending. They talked for about two hours and then he returned to Shanghai by car at about 11 AM. Break in the Kidnapping Case in Jiaodiaowan: The military police investigation unit has solved the kidnapping case in Yin Xietai's Caofang store in Jiaodiaowan, the tenth district of the county. At about 9 PM on the 10th of this month, six armed robbers broke into the store, entered the room, and robbed seventy-five dollars in cash, a pair of gold earrings, and abducted Yin Qiuyun's two-year-old son, Zilin, before heading west. On the 18th, the family received a letter from the bandits demanding a ransom of 5,000 yuan and requesting contact in Shanghai. The victim had no choice but to report the incident to the military police investigation unit in Songjiang. Chief Detective Yang Shijie was immediately dispatched to accompany the victim to Shanghai to report the incident to the police. At 1 AM on the 27th, they successfully apprehended a female bandit, Wu Lushi, and rescued the hostage, Pan Yaqiu, near the entrance of the Great World Hotel. They immediately returned to Songjiang by an early train. Under interrogation, the female bandit confessed to guarding the hostage. She has been handed over to the county government for trial.

Suzhou 64

A Strange Tale of Polydactyly in Two Sons: Gu, a villager from Beijie Township in Dongqiao Township of the county, has two sons. The elder son, Peiji, is ten years old and has twelve fingers on his hands and fourteen toes on his feet. The younger son, Peifang, is two years old and has twenty-four fingers and toes. Yesterday (the 29th), they were sent to the Boxi Hospital in the city to have the conjoined fingers surgically separated.

Team Leader Du Injured in Bandit Attack: Du Jingwu, the leader of the first squad of the 14th Water Police Team in Wujiang, has been diligently suppressing bandits and has captured countless lake bandits. He recently escorted Liu Xueshi, Wang Heshang, and seven others, who were also captured by Du, to the provincial security office where they were executed last Saturday. As a result, the lake bandits have harbored deep resentment. After the death of Squadron Leader Huai Zongbang of the 14th Team recently, the district chief Gong appointed Du as the acting squadron leader of the 14th Team. On the 28th, Du received intelligence that a large gang of lake bandits had been spotted in the Miaogang area. He immediately led three patrol boats from his first squad and three patrol boats from the second squad to search and suppress them, but they encountered nothing. After returning, he stayed overnight at the first squad headquarters outside the north gate of Wujiang. However, at 2:30 AM yesterday (the 28th), seventy to eighty lake bandits from Haizhou and Henan suddenly arrived on eight boats from Taihu Lake and the canal. After landing, they surrounded the squad headquarters and attacked, vowing revenge. As a result, Team Leader Du was shot three times in his right lower leg, shattering the bone. A bullet also passed through the left side of his face. Afterwards, County Magistrate Wu Jia of Wujiang hired a steamboat to send him to the Suzhou Tianci and Boxi Hospitals for treatment. Because Du himself is unable to speak, details about the damage to the weaponry of the squad headquarters are temporarily difficult to obtain.

Kunshan 65

Mother and Son Both Die After Failed Speculation: Dong Xiangfu, originally from Xugongqiao West Village in the third district, opened the Dachengde flower rice store in Minhang and also independently established the Xiangji Grain Box store on Baoshan Street in Shanghai. His family mostly resides in Shanghai, with only his elderly mother and a maid in the countryside. Dong learned of his mother's illness in early August and returned home. Before leaving, he instructed a friend, Jia, to purchase ten cartloads of wheat futures (500 dan per cart) at the exchange and made arrangements with a Qianzhuang (money shop) to pay the margin. Unexpectedly, Jia predicted that the price of wheat would rise and doubled the purchase without informing Dong. Currently, the market has fallen, resulting in significant losses. A few days ago, the Qianzhuang sent a clerk to the countryside to demand payment from Dong. Only then did Dong learn the full story. At that time, Dong's mother's illness had slightly improved, but she was greatly shocked and fearful upon hearing that her son had lost a large sum of money, causing her condition to worsen again. The next morning, she passed away. Dong, grieving greatly for his mother's death, suffered a recurrence of his old liver and stomach ailment and died eight hours later, following his mother to the underworld. Those who heard of this were saddened.

Fengxian 66

Zhao Jingyi and Daughter Kidnapped En Route: Zhao Jingyi, who runs an oil press in Hujiaqiao, has been in decline since being kidnapped and ransomed two years ago due to excessive losses. This time, Zhao's mother was taking her daughter to Shanghai yesterday to buy her trousseau. Unexpectedly, while passing through Shagang, they were stopped by several bandits who kidnapped Zhao's mother and daughter from the boat. The boatman swam back to report the incident. A search was launched, but there was no trace of the bandits.

Regulations on Fines Published in Table Form: Li Zhibin, Chief of the County Public Security Bureau, stated that fines for violations of regulations at each branch bureau should be handled in accordance with judicial regulations. Therefore, he issued an order yesterday to all branch bureaus stating that starting next month, for all violation cases, in addition to separately submitting the fines as required and awarding bonuses, they should also list the cause of the case, name, amount of fine, violated regulations, and serial number, and report them to the General Bureau for review, sealing, and public announcement to ensure transparency.

Wujiang 67

Difficulties in Converting Field Tax from Taels to Yuan: The province has ordered the conversion of field tax from taels to yuan in the county and instructed the county to implement it. The county finance bureau has sent personnel to Kunshan to investigate, but that county has no specific measures either. Furthermore, this county has more than 430,000 households paying the grain tax, and the taxation rules of the old Jiangzhen areas are different. The procedures for verification and registration are cumbersome, so it is impossible to handle them in time for the busy tax season. A request has now been submitted to the Department of Finance for approval to postpone the implementation.

Wuxi 68

Construction Committee Plans to Build Large Gaoqiao Power Plant: In order to develop the domestic electrical industry, the Construction Committee of the National Government plans to build a large power plant near Gaoqiao outside the north gate of the county. A surveying team from the Taihu Water Conservancy Committee was dispatched by the committee a week ago to Wuxi to conduct precise surveys. As of the day before yesterday, the surveying team had completed all the surveying work. Once the construction plan is drawn up, land will be acquired, requiring about forty to fifty mu. The construction cost is estimated at two million yuan. The Construction Committee had previously submitted a request to the National Government to allocate forty million yuan from the returned Boxer Indemnity funds to develop the electrical industry and construct water conservancy projects nationwide. The funds required to build the power plant are planned to be drawn from this allocation. At the same time, the Ministry of Railways also plans to add a small station between Wuxi and Shitangwan. Upon hearing this news, the Construction Committee wrote to the Ministry of Railways requesting that the small station between Shitangwan be located at Gaoqiao to facilitate the transportation of coal after the Gaoqiao power plant is built. The Ministry of Railways then instructed Liu Weichi, Director of the Jinghu Railway Bureau, to send personnel to Wuxi to conduct a survey in conjunction with Wu Yulin, Director of the Qishuyan Power Plant, and it has been decided to build the station at Gaoqiao.

Theft and Injury in Qingsong Township: Zhang Shiheng (also known as Ren Gen), a resident of Qingsong Township near Zhang Jingqiao in the seventh district (Huai Shangshi) of the county, works as a farmer. At about 1 AM the night before last, seven or eight bandits wearing white cloths on their heads and carrying guns and wooden sticks broke open the front door and entered. They immediately tied up Shiheng and his eldest son, A-Zi, with ropes and beat them severely with the backs of knives and wooden sticks, causing both father and son to be covered in injuries. The bandits then ransacked the house, searching at will. After an hour, they left with their loot. Upon inspection, it was found that they had stolen 141 yuan in silver dollars, 70 yuan in banknotes, three gold rings, a pair of gold bracelets, and clothing, worth about 300 yuan.

Large Number of Refugees Disturb Fengxiang: At about 10:30 AM yesterday (September 29th), more than 400 refugees, men, women, old, and young, from Changsha, Hunan, suddenly arrived at Fengxiang in the fourth district (Kaiyuan Township) of the county. The refugee leaders, Hu Huicun and Zheng Huanzhang, dispatched five or six refugees to the ninth branch of the public security bureau, requesting food and other supplies. Liu, the chief of the branch bureau, granted their request. However, a group of refugees began to cause disturbances at the home of Feng Zhaoqiu, a resident of the alley. After the villagers reported this to the township office, the office reported it to the county government. County Magistrate Pan, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered Wang Weili, the commander of the police brigade, to dispatch armed soldiers to suppress the disturbance. Only then did the refugees stop causing further trouble.

Urgency in Constructing the Ring-Lake Road: Previously, the Jiangsu Provincial Government considered that Taihu Lake, spanning three provinces (Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui), has long been a haven for bandits. Even though government police actively suppressed them, it was only a temporary measure and failed to fundamentally eliminate the problem. It was decided at a provincial government meeting to start with construction and build a ring-lake road. The Department of Construction was to draw up a plan for the entire route, starting from Yixing, connecting to the Ninghang Road, passing through Wujin, Wuxi, Wuxian, and Pingwang in Wujiang, and reaching Nanxun in Zhejiang. The Department of Construction has dispatched Sun Baoqin, the leader of the surveying team of the Provincial Highway Bureau, to conduct the survey. It was decided to start the survey in Wuxi. Sun has arrived in Wuxi and is working actively with six surveyors and more than twenty laborers. They started with Yuantouzhu in Kaiyuan Township, Southern Spring and Xin'an in Kaihua, and Nanwangting in Wuxian County, then to Wangting, Jinshu, Guangfu, and Mudu, and finally to Suzhou, a total of over 140 kilometers. The entire survey has been completed. The team has traveled to Suzhou to continue the survey. The total cost of the entire ring-lake road project is estimated at 1.975 million yuan and has been allocated from the 7 million yuan construction bonds recently issued by the Jiangsu province.

Striving to Retain Grain Tax for Local Expenses: This year's winter grain tax has been ordered to be increased by two yuan. However, it was previously approved that one-quarter be retained by the county and divided to be used for various local expenses, but this year, no explicit order has been designated. Lu Renshou, Director of the County Education Bureau, yesterday met with the County Finance Management Office, the Construction Bureau, and the Sericulture Farm to request the county government to submit a report to the Department of Finance and Education to allocate the five jiao retained by the county to local projects, and to send a letter to the education bureaus of other counties to fight for it.

Changzhou 69

Xue Yongda's Son Kidnapped in the Fifth District: Last night, six bandits broke into Xue Yongda's house in Xuejiatou, Dingtang Township, in the fifth district of Wuyi. They climbed over the wall, broke into the room, and kidnapped Yongda's son without stealing anything else. They only left a note demanding a ransom. They then left.

Changshu 70

New and Old Supervision Committee Members Handover: Since the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department designated Wu Zhongying, Xu Jiugong, and Shen Zuguang as members of the county party department and Shi Minyong as supervisor, they have not yet formally assumed their duties. The inauguration ceremony and the handover between the new and old members are scheduled for the morning of the 29th of this month. A request has been submitted to the province to send personnel to oversee the ceremony.

Telephone Dispute Remains Unresolved: The local telephone company's dispute with users over price increases has lasted for more than two months. The Ministry of Communications ordered the county to work with the director of the telegraph bureau to mediate, and the two sides were gradually approaching an agreement. However, recently, a dispute arose in Suzhou, causing the negotiations to stall again. Yesterday, the Telephone User Association held a committee meeting and decided to: (1) Notify all users to temporarily suspend payment of monthly telephone fees until the matter is resolved because the county government is currently handling the matter; (2) Send an official letter to the county government to inquire about County Magistrate Tan's plan to handle the dispute, and then hold another meeting.

County Magistrate Investigates Ayu Fish Mouth: Ayu Fish Mouth, under the jurisdiction of the first district of the county, is an important passage from Yangcheng Lake to Huxupu, Xuliujing, Gaopukou, and other seaports. The district affairs meeting previously resolved to seal off Ayu Fish Mouth to block the routes of bandits. The decision was submitted to the county for implementation. It has now been learned that County Magistrate Tan believes it is necessary to investigate whether there is a need to seal off Ayu Fish Mouth, so he instructed the Construction Bureau to quickly investigate the area and report back.

Jiangyin 71

The Agricultural Bank's Funding Fell Short of the Quota, Making it Difficult to Follow Established Precedent: The County Rectification Committee Previously Submitted to the Provincial Rectification Committee, Citing the Precedent of Wuxi, to Raise 100,000 Yuan for Loans to Farmers. The Provincial Rectification Committee Approved a Reply from the Provincial Government's Letter Approving the Agricultural and Mining Bureau. According to the Agricultural Bank's Reply, Wuxi's Submitted Agricultural Bank Funding had Exceeded 60%, So the Bank established a Branch there, and agricultural loans are handled by the branch. The head office has not made large loans, so it is unknown what Jiangyin Party Rectification Committee based its statement on. As of recently, Jiangyin had only submitted over 46,000 Yuan, which is below the standard for establishing a branch. Once the submitted funding reaches the quota, a branch can be established, and all loans can be implemented, so it is said.

Difficult to Donate Funds Due to Counter-Revolutionary Case: Former Municipal Administrative Bureau Chief Ji Hehua was arrested and detained due to counter-revolutionary relations. His father, Ji Ziqing, tried every means to rescue him and was willing to donate 3,000 Yuan to purchase guns for the Self-Defense Corps. His submitted document requesting this was met with the response that his son, Ji Hehua, had been arrested on suspicion of banditry, and if the investigation found counter-revolutionary facts, he would be subject to legal sanctions and would not be easily let off. If the investigation found no connection, he would be exempt from prosecution and released, without needing your donation to supplement military equipment. Await the government's investigation and handle it according to law. Bandits Rob Self-Defense Corps Firearms: Banditry in the west of the county had subsided slightly after two large-scale searches and suppressions by the Chengwu Joint Defense Military Police. Recently, it suddenly became rampant again. The night before last (the 27th), bandits led by Gao Xiaosheng, a primary school student, robbed 37 firearms from the Self-Defense Corps in Qianzhou Huang Village. The Sixth Branch of the Sixth District Post dispatched police to counterattack and repel them. Yesterday, Liu Zuigeng, the district chief of the Sixth District, reported to the county in the city and dispatched a team to the countryside to garrison and take the opportunity to search and suppress.

The Self-Defense Corps Captured Thieves and Handed Them Over to the County: The Zhouzhuang Township Self-Defense Corps captured Li Ruren, the father of the concubine of bandit Lu Zhanglin (whose daughter was previously captured in Suzhou), in Xishi a few days ago and handed him over to the county on the 28th. Also, a few days ago, they captured Xu Zini, Zhou Aliu, and Xu Axi, who lived in Xuxiang Lane, because they were involved in a robbery case in the eastern township, and handed them over to the county for interrogation.

Nantong 72

Li Mingyang Reports on Suppressing Communists and Bandits: In the past year, the counties of Tong, Ru, Hai, Tai, and Jing in northern Jiangsu Province have become havens for communists and bandits, causing great harm. On the 10th of this month, Security Director Li Mingyang, led the security regiment from the province to Taixing Huangqiao to supervise the suppression. As of the 27th, the suppression was implemented. On the 28th, he and Secretary Feng Peisan came to Tong. At 1:00 PM, people from all walks of life held a welcome meeting at the club. Mr. Li reported on the suppression of communists and bandits in Tongtai, stating that the bandit suppression plan was decided at the Tongtai Six County Defense and Suppression Conference on August 20th. Since the main gathering place of communists and bandits was in Taixing, they started with Tai first. The Tongtai area is near the river with many branches, making it easy for bandits to appear and disappear. Moreover, the counties had not experienced war for decades or centuries, and the people had no self-defense organizations. When an incident happened suddenly, it quickly spread like wildfire. The Communist Party colluded with bandits. The bandit pseudo-command headquarters in Huangqiao had a military commission and a violent commission, and their only tactic was to coerce farmers and workers. Their slogan was "roll people." In the Huangqiao battle a few days ago, the bandit crowd was said to be 10,000, but only 600 or so had guns. They collapsed after attacking for more than ten minutes. He immediately implemented both suppression and appeasement. Those who were coerced surrendered their weapons and surrendered. The Communist Party knew it was difficult to gain a foothold and fled. Bandits were resolved within ten days by Li Jigen, who surrendered, recruited more than 3,000 bandits. The territory of Tongtai was immediately pacified. In the future, local self-defense strength needs to be supplemented and a fundamental solution sought. Director Li went to suppress Ma Yuren's troops along the coastal area of Yancheng, which were unusually rampant, on the 29th with the 3rd Security Regiment.

Wounded Soldiers Leave Tong for Pukou: Commander-in-Chief sent committee members Shao Weihan and Huang Zhuojie to Tong to handle the discharge of wounded soldiers from the 31st Rear Hospital. There are more than 1,000 wounded soldiers. Each person was given 8 yuan for returning to the team, and they took a boat from Tianshenggang to Pukou to return to the front line.

Rugao 73

What I Heard About the Beloved Concubine's Suicide: Xia Guangyu, former executive committee member and training director of the Rugao County Party Department, and current director of the Infant Care Center of the County Relief Institute, lives in West Main Street in the city. Last year, he took a concubine, surnamed Gu, named Zicui, 18 years old, petite and exquisite, with beautiful appearance, the daughter of a tenant farmer surnamed Gu of the Infant Care Center in Shili Pu in the urban area. She has been with Xia for a year. At first, she was placed in a "golden house" at the Third Company in Zhang Family Ancestral Hall, Hexi, West Gate. Recently, she was taken back to live with the main wife (Gu Chengzhi's daughter). On the 22nd night, the concubine suddenly hanged herself. Xia hid the body in the suite. Unexpectedly, the matter was not kept secret. Last night (the 24th), the town office clerks of the town found out and reported it to the town office, and the town office reported it to the county government. So Xia also asked the county government for an examination. Now the front and back of Xia's house have been guarded by police. This matter has caused a sensation throughout the city, and people are flocking to see it. As of the time the reporter was writing, there were no results from the examination. It is said that the deceased was pregnant and was due this month. Because she could not bear the abuse of the main wife, she committed suicide in anger. Now the neighbors will also present it to the county government for examination to clarify the matter.

Two Bandits Captured in the Case of the Li Family Father and Son Burned to Death: During May of this year, more than a dozen bandits came to the house of Li Tingyao, a farmer in the ninth district of this county, and robbed clothes, jewelry, and silver dollars worth more than 1,000 yuan, and subjected him to torture, burning an iron pot red and tying Tingyao and his son to the pot to burn them to death. Later, Li Enming, Tingyao's nephew, reported the case to the county government, which sent personnel to verify that it was true. Thorough Investigation of Embezzlement of Construction Funds: The construction funds of Jiangsu Province are very large, and they are mostly mixed up between the Finance and Construction Bureaus. Recently, the director of the Jurong County Construction Bureau reported to Director Sun Hongji of the Construction Bureau that the county Finance Bureau had reduced the amount of funds allocated to the bureau. He also said that a lot of the county's construction funds had been embezzled. After receiving the report, Director Sun sent Liu Gonghe, an inspector from the bureau, to conduct a thorough investigation. Liu discovered that Zhou Shoulin, the director of the Jurong Finance Bureau, had embezzled funds twice, totaling more than 7,000 yuan. He took the documents back to the bureau and reported to Director Sun, who was very angry. He proposed at the provincial government meeting to dismiss Zhou as director and put him under surveillance. The Finance Bureau would send personnel to jointly re-investigate. If there were no differences, he would send personnel to take over the duties of the Jurong Finance Bureau and order former Director Zhou to hand over more than 2,000 yuan in water conservancy funds to the Construction Bureau, and other funds would be handled separately when the old and new directors handed over their duties. Director Sun was afraid that similar incidents might occur in other counties, so he sent personnel to various counties to investigate and found that a total of 350,000 yuan had been embezzled. Since it was related to construction, he drafted a five-part form for approval and implementation to prevent further embezzlement and fraud.

Su Yi Education Office

Holding Cooperative Agricultural Experiment Fields 81

Location: Zhongleng New Village, Zhenjiang

The Jiangsu Provincial Preparatory Office for United Compulsory Education has established an experimental zone for popular education (Zhongleng New Village, Zhenjiang). The main crops in the area are rice and wheat, but due to poor varieties and poor planting methods, the results are declining. The office is now responsible for guiding agricultural improvement and education. It has now signed a contract with Lu Yueting, a resident of the area, to conduct a cooperative agricultural experiment field. The method is to divide the farmland into two equal areas, A and B. Area A is still cultivated freely by the owner, and Area B is also cultivated by the owner, but the planting method must be guided by the experimental zone and cannot be changed without authorization. The taxes to be paid each year for the guided area will be borne by the experimental zone, and the products will belong to the owner to compensate for the extra labor. If the harvest in Area B is less than Area A, the experimental zone will compensate for the difference. The seeds and fertilizers used will be introduced by the Popular Education Experimental Zone. The experimental methods, such as labor, seeds, fertilizers, and crop growth and harvest, will be recorded using scientific methods on a regular basis for verification. With this method, the owners can have no unexpected losses, and the area can obtain the convenience of the experiment with very little expense. If rural primary schools in various places can follow this method, the future of agriculture will inevitably improve universally, and people's livelihood education will be easier to start.

Recent News from the Sino-French University in Lyon 82

Since its establishment by Cai Zimin and others in the tenth year of the Republic of China, the Sino-French University in Lyon has been in operation for less than ten years. The number of students admitted has not exceeded 300. However, the overall results are quite impressive. Since the opening of the school, a total of 39 students have obtained doctoral degrees (15 in science, 9 in humanities, 6 in medicine, 2 in pharmacy, and 7 in law), 30 students have obtained master's degrees (27 in science and 3 in humanities), 28 students have obtained engineering degrees (12 in engineering, 6 in chemistry, 7 in electrical engineering, and 1 each in mining, leather making, and papermaking), 36 higher diplomas and 176 higher certificates have been obtained in various schools, and 26 first prizes, medals, and certificates have been obtained in art schools, architecture schools, and conservatories of music. One person has graduated from the Paris Polytechnic School and two have graduated from the Three-Tin Army School. All these results are based on what can be calculated. As for the special research done by the students, those who reported at the French National Doctoral Association and their personal works published in various journals are too numerous to mention.

Guanlan Compulsory Education Experimental Zone Plan 85

The Baoshan Education Sector specially established the Guanlan Compulsory Education Experimental Zone to commemorate Yuan Guanlan. It was announced at the memorial service the day before yesterday. The plan is excerpted as follows:

(1) Location: Mr. Yuan dedicated his life to education, and all his achievements need no further description. However, he especially promoted compulsory education and devoted the most energy to it. Fulfilling Mr. Yuan's unfinished ambition is the responsibility of those who died later. This is why Mr. Jiang Wenyu and others advocated holding the Guantan Compulsory Education Experimental Zone as a spiritual memorial. Mr. Yuan grew up in Baoyi. Baoyi formerly had two townships, Yuepu and Liuhang. The educational foundation is better than other cities and villages. Five years ago, the public proposed to designate the Zhenxin and Juquan schools in the two townships as model schools and provided funds to enrich the content in order to lay the foundation for promoting compulsory education. Although education in the two townships has been promoted every year, it has not reached the goal of universal education due to limited financial resources. Compared with the two townships, Liuhang is more convenient for transportation, has a smaller area, and has fewer students, making it easier to start promoting compulsory education. Therefore, the former Liuhang Township was selected as the Guanlan Compulsory Education Experimental Zone. (2) Number of existing schools in Liuhang Township: There are 10 schools in Liuhang Township. The distance between each school is mostly within three miles, and rarely outside three miles. In the future, the promotion only needs to add grades to the existing schools, without having to set up more schools. (3) Number of students in Liuhang Township: According to the report of the Baoshan County Education Bureau in the 18th year, the total number of students in Liuhang Township is more than 2,100, and the number of students who have not attended school is more than 1,450. (4) The distribution of existing schools and children who have not attended school in Liuhang is shown in the left picture (omitted). Explanation 1: Assuming that each level of promotion accommodates 50 students, then to achieve universal education in the whole township, about 30 levels need to be promoted. 1. According to the standard of additional class funding stipulated by the Baoshan County Education Bureau, the start-up cost for each level is 150 yuan and the regular cost is 316 yuan. Then, to add 30 levels, the start-up cost is about 4,500 yuan and the regular cost is 9,500 yuan. It is not easy to seek universal education in the whole township without raising a fund of 100,000 yuan. (5) Implementation steps: The steps to promote compulsory education must be based on economic talents, so the scope of the experimental area should not be too large in the initial stage, otherwise it will not be easy to maintain if it is not economical, that is, the talent is not enough to allocate. It is now assumed that there are two implementation steps with a fund of 30,000 yuan and 50,000 yuan. With the fund of 30,000 yuan, the interest of about 3,000 yuan can be obtained. According to the above-mentioned standard of additional class funding, about 10 levels can be promoted, accommodating 500 students. The experimental area is located in the 7th District near the Juquan Central Primary School because of its convenient transportation, and the Juquan School is the central agency for research and guidance. It is planned to promote it in two steps, as shown on the left (with a map of the experimental area) (omitted). Supplementary explanation: Every poor child in the countryside cannot attend school all day because of subsidies for family homework. If four-tenths of the funds can be used to set up half-day classes, in addition to setting up six full-day classes, eight half-day classes can be obtained, increasing by four classes, and accommodating 200 more students. First, the 25th District (69 students) and the 12th District (161 students) will be drawn into the experimental area, as shown in the attached figure (omitted). Yi Fund 50,000 yuan, an annual interest of approximately 5,000 yuan can be obtained, which can promote 16 levels and accommodate approximately 800 students. The experimental area is also centered on the Juquan Central Primary School, and it is planned to promote it in three steps, as shown in the table on the left (omitted). Supplementary explanation: If four-tenths of the funds can be used to set up half-day classes, then in addition to the ten full-day classes, twelve half-day classes can be obtained, an increase of six classes, and 300 more students can be accommodated. The 12th District (161 students), the 11th District of Dongtian (73 students), and the 47th District (113 students) will be drawn into the experimental area. The attached figure is as follows (omitted). Promoting compulsory education is not only about expanding the quantity, but also about improving the quality. In the future, there should be a considerable organization for research and guidance on the implementation. The plan will be determined separately.

National Sports Federation Registration Issue 86

Director Wang Zhengting Goes to Beijing to Explain

The China National Amateur Athletic Federation previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Interior of the National Government for registration, but it has not yet been approved. Meanwhile, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has issued several directives urging the National Sports Federation to register with the bureau first. The federation ignored these directives. The Bureau of Education then requested instructions from the Ministry of Education as to whether the federation should register with the Bureau of Education first. The Ministry of Education instructed the bureau, stating, "The submitted documents and attachments have been reviewed. Article 1 of the 'Measures for Educational Administrative Organs to Manage Academic Groups' stipulates that an academic group, in addition to complying with the General Principles of the Civil Code and other laws and regulations, shall handle matters in accordance with these measures." Furthermore, Item 7 of Section 3 of the revised 'Organizational Plan for People's Groups' stipulates, "Social groups with special legal provisions shall comply with the provisions of special laws." Since the China National Amateur Athletic Federation is an academic group in nature, it should, in addition to fulfilling other required procedures, submit a registration application to the bureau in accordance with the 'Measures for Educational Administrative Organs to Manage Academic Groups.' The request to forward a consultation to the Ministry of Interior for clarification should not be considered." The National Sports Federation held a meeting of its executive directors on the evening of the 28th at the Tao Le Chun Restaurant on San Ma Road. Those present included Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting and Zhao Jinqing. Regarding the federation's registration issue, Foreign Minister Wang stated that it should not register with the Bureau of Education, saying, "The Bureau of Education is responsible for all matters related to 'education,' while the National Sports Federation is outside the scope of 'education' and is an organization that enables those who have received education to engage in technical competitions based on their usual training." Foreign Minister Wang has now taken the Bureau of Education's directive to Nanjing to explain everything directly to the Ministry of Interior.

Tie Mingde Receives Honor at International Soil Congress 88

At this year's International Soil Congress held in Moscow, Russia, our country did not attend due to various reasons, but only sent reports and other materials. It is now learned that the congress has elected our country's member Tie Mingde as an honorary member, because his published research on soil ultrafine particles is extremely valuable.

It is said that Tie is a native of Shanghai, studied soil science in the United States, and served as a soil science technician at the Oregon State Experiment Station in the United States, a technician at the Guangxi Agricultural Bureau, and a section chief at the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining Inspection Institute. His research on ultrafine particles began when he was in Oregon. After returning to China, he revised and referenced his findings multiple times before publishing them.

Lehua Team This Season 97

Still a Question of Joining the Westerners' Football Club, Expected to Return to Shanghai Today or October 2nd

The China Expeditionary Football Team organized by the Lehua Sports Association, due to procedural errors, failed to fulfill its ambitions and its grand plan was suspended. It returned to the country by ship from Singapore on the 20th of this month and is expected to arrive in port today. There is also an unconfirmed report that it will arrive on October 2nd. The biggest problem after the team's arrival is whether the team can still participate in various competitions of the Westerners' Football Club. The Westerners' Club has only given the word "provisional" to Lehua's application to join Group A. This word has a deep meaning. Sun Guiyun Engaged 98

Swimming Nearly Drowned

Mr. Xu Selflessly Rescues

Miss's Heart Lingers

Reported As Gratitude

Ms. Sun Guiyun, a nationally famous female sprinter, recently nearly drowned while practicing swimming. She was rescued by a student from Northeastern University and did not end up being buried in the belly of a fish. Ms. Sun was so grateful that she felt she could not repay the kindness even by working like a horse, so she vowed to repay with her body. This issue, which has always been of concern, has been resolved. Those who admired Ms. Sun very much at the National Games in Hangzhou in the past are all surprised. After the closing of the 9th Far Eastern Games, Ms. Sun returned to Harbin from Japan. Having been stimulated, she was determined to practice hard and aspired to be an all-around athlete in all sports. Ms. Sun is very interested in swimming and practices very hard. One day, while practicing swimming in a newly built swimming pool in a park, she was careless and was in danger of joining the water gods. While struggling, she shouted for help. Mr. Xu, a student from Northeastern University, heard the call, found her, and rescued her at the risk of his own life. She was lucky to escape. The two developed feelings for each other, which was the beginning. Later, after spending a long time together, they became even closer. Sun was promised to marry, hoping to spend a happy life together. It is said that Ms. Sun's wedding is scheduled for the spring. Mrs. Yu Fengzhi, the wife of Zhang Xueliang, is quite friendly with Sun. When Sun holds her wedding ceremony in the future, she will invite Commander Zhang Xueliang to be the officiant.

All Circles Prepare for National Day Commemoration 108

Outline of Measures Passed

The Municipal Executive Committee, recognizing that the National Day commemoration is imminent, convened the Shanghai Municipal All Circles Commemoration Preparatory Committee, consisting of various agencies and organizations, to prepare for the celebration. The committee held its first meeting on the third floor of the Municipal Party Headquarters the day before yesterday. The representatives present were Li Zheng from the Municipal Propaganda Department, Hou Dachun from the Civil Training Association, Zhu Jiaxiang from the Municipal Training Department, Chen Baolian from the Municipal Secretariat, Chen Kecheng from the Municipal Government, Zhang Taiji from the Garrison Headquarters, Ni Guangzu from the Shanghai Special District Local Court, Xu Shijin from the Health Bureau, Chen Maoxian from the Naval Headquarters, Wang Penggou from the Shanghai Local Court, Cao Sunguo from the Public Works Bureau, Wang Keyong from the Education Bureau, Zhou Yongxing from the Social Affairs Bureau, Xu Zuyin from the Second Branch of the High Court, Gong Yushuo from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, He Xiaosong from the Jianghai Customs Superintendent, Min Luobing from the Two Roads Party Headquarters, Zhang Xianfang from the Citizens' Union, Jiang Yuhua from the Women's Association, Zheng Chengqing from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Tan Bozhi from the Railway Bureau, Kuang Yunwen from the Arsenal, Chen Xinghan from the Two Roads Railway Bureau, Wu Yinchun, Zhu Shujian, Li Chunshen, Yang Shaozhi, Shen Ding, Shen Yu, Yang Youren, Shen Risheng, and Wang Zhijian from the district party headquarters, Zhu Airen and others from the Second Directly Subordinate Branch, totaling 33 people. Hou Dachun chaired the meeting and reported on the significance of commemorating National Day. He also stated that with the collapse of Yan and Feng and the unification being imminent, it is appropriate to celebrate with a grand event to show public opinion. Then, the organizational outline of the committee and the outline of the National Day celebration measures passed by the Municipal Executive Committee were approved. The following temporary motions were made: (1) Determine the budget for the committee. Resolved: The chairman will prepare a budget of income and expenditure and submit it to the second meeting on Wednesday for discussion. (2) Determine the location of the committee's office. Resolved: The third floor of the Municipal Party Headquarters. (3) The location of the committee's entertainment fair is the Municipal Public Sports Field. There is a conflict between the athletic games held on that day and the committee's various celebration times. How should this be handled? Resolved: Send a letter to the Education Bureau ordering the athletic games hosted by the field to be held elsewhere. (4) Should the celebration meeting be held in different districts? Resolved: Submit to the Standing Committee for discussion. (5) Elect Comrade Hou Dachun as chairman of the committee and Comrade Li Zheng as a member of the Standing Committee of the committee. Resolved: Passed. The meeting adjourned.

The first meeting of the Standing Committee was convened yesterday, chaired by Hou Dachun. The matters discussed were as follows: (1) Appoint the heads and deputy heads of each department. (2) The chairman prepares a budget of income and expenditure for review. Resolved: Revise and submit to the preparatory committee for review. (3) Broadly raise funds. (4) The Entertainment Department proposed that the committee should convene people from the entertainment industry to hold a discussion meeting to promote progress. Resolved: The discussion meeting will be held on the afternoon of October 3rd at the Hua An Building. (5) Should the general assembly be held in different districts? Resolved: Hold it in 15 districts, with a subsidy of 20 yuan per district. Temporary motion: Determine the date of the second meeting. Resolved: It will be held at 10:00 AM on October 2nd. The meeting adjourned.
