Youth Garden

Impressions of a Northern Tour (8) 249

— Su Ling

Sowing Seeds in the Desert

Sowing seeds in the desert? Who in the world would do such a thing? Gull (Note) says, "Sowing seeds in the desert is a great undertaking because it is difficult, and therefore the cause is great and necessary."

How dare we accept such praise? We only wish to be a part of humanity, to dedicate ourselves to art, to fulfill a small part of our responsibility to our culturally backward nation, struggling with our own suffering, and sowing a few seeds here and there. Moreover, the deformed society often disappoints, disheartens, and even corrupts many sincere workers...

The emptiness of the content of this Harbin city, which is merely decorated with a magnificent exterior, will disappoint you as if you had stepped into an empty tomb that has been excavated.

Although those buildings stand tall, apart from the stores that are piled high with imported foreign goods, what about the cultural associations, libraries...? Of course, they also support some diners. There are also many secondary schools and higher schools, which accommodate many young people... In short, everything is just a decoration on the outside. Moreover, the cultural association is run by the Japanese. The so-called Sino-Russian joint industrial university is staffed by Russian professors, and all courses are printed in Russian. Naturally, it is not surprising that an industrial university student once asked someone, "Do universities in China, such as those in Beijing and Shanghai, use Chinese textbooks?"

Harbin's lack of cultural development has its reasons. In the past, it was a Russian concession, and all facilities were Russian. If there was culture, it was Russian culture. The concession was taken back. It is said that in the past two years, there has indeed been more cultural development, but everything is empty and not progressing... The reason is the political oppression and the practitioners' deception and selfishness towards the cause.

Engaging in cultural undertakings in Harbin is indeed urgently needed, and what is needed is enlightenment work, starting from sowing seeds. Gull says, "Harbin's culture is so desolate, especially the literary and artistic circles, which are simply still in the wilderness, in the desert. However, sowing seeds in the desert..." Naturally, we are starting to cultivate this wilderness, sowing seeds in this desert.

I am very happy that I have wandered far away to the frontier, and it is not entirely useless, but at the same time I feel ashamed. Is what I know enough to teach others? How should I cautiously strive?

"Comrades, let's all work hard, work hard for culture, and create a glorious responsibility for all the backward nations, which rests on our shoulders!"

The first time I met a group of young art students of my age, I said this to them.

(Note) Gull is a newly acquainted friend after touring the north. He is a Cantonese expatriate living in Harbin.

The Race Before Class 250

— Quan

Jiaotong University Female Students Newly Moved Dormitory Distance Too Far Practice Racing

The female dormitory of Jiaotong University was originally in a two-story foreign house. Although the foreign house was not large, it was beautifully constructed and was the former residence of the president. Moreover, the number of female students was not large (only sixteen in the previous semester), so it was suitable for living in. After the start of this semester, the school authorities, because the president's family had to move into the school and it was inconvenient for the female students to occupy the president's residence, and the number of female students had increased this semester, the original dormitory felt very cramped. The Department of Training and Education repeatedly planned, but could not find a suitable place, because the planned South Court was still borrowed by the Nanyang Model Primary and Secondary School. Later, it was decided to move the faculty and staff in the East Dormitory to the remaining fifteen rooms in Zhixin West Hall (Zhixin West Hall was occupied by the third and fourth grades of the school, and was luxuriously built, with fifteen rooms vacant this semester), and move all the female students into the East Dormitory. The East Dormitory faces a small stream in front and vacant land in the back (South Court Playground). The freshness of the air goes without saying. Moreover, the house is a Western-style new building originally built by the family of Sheng, a student of the school's primary school, specifically for his son to live in. After his son dropped out of school, he donated it to the school, so it is extraordinarily beautiful and has a small playground where one can exercise a little. Because it is located in the eastern corner, there are very few students coming and going, so one can play freely, unlike the shyness of being under the gaze of male students before. However, although the East Dormitory has many advantages, it is not without its shortcomings. Because the East Dormitory is located in the eastern corner, it is very far from the Middle Court and Upper Court (where the classrooms are located), and even further from the laboratory and radio station. It takes a lot of time to go back and forth to the dormitory after class, and it is definitely not possible to go back and forth in the ten-minute break. Therefore, in order to adapt to the environment, the female students had to implement a running plan. Every time after class, a group of women in long robes and short hair were seen running in a line on the playground, with neat steps and not slow speed. From a distance, it looked like swallows flying across the sky. In an instant, the large playground had been crossed. After crossing the playground, there was still a distance of five hundred meters. In total, from the Middle Court to the dormitory, it was about six hundred and fifty meters. Starting from the Upper Court, it was even further. Therefore, female students have to run at least 1,300 meters each time they return to the dormitory. It is said that a female student in the school who is good at sports said that if this continues, all the female students in the school will become long-distance runners. However, a few students bought bicycles to replace walking, which can also create a new record for riding bicycles, it is said.

Youth Garden Submission Guidelines 251

(1) The text should be within the scope of discussions on youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, etc., and the style is not limited.

(2) The pictures should be limited to those related to youth issues.

Shanghai Market

Market News 252

Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau at the intersection of Shilu and Sanma Road announced that since the opening of the bureau, the business has been exceptionally developed, and the newly decorated items have even wider sales, because the products are exquisite and the patterns are novel. The bureau recently sent personnel to major famous factories in Suzhou, Hangzhou and other places to order a large batch of fashionable silks and satins, which were transported to the display windows yesterday for people to visit. The novelty of the patterns, the gorgeousness of the colors, and the firmness of the texture will surely win the hearts of the society. Ladies from all walks of life who want to buy cheap and beautiful silks and satins, this is a good opportunity, etc., etc.

Construction Book Bureau announced that in order to meet local needs, the bureau has specially set up a distribution office in the middle city of Bai'er Road, which opened the day before yesterday (28th) and is very busy, especially the sales of stationery are huge. Books from major bookstores in this port are available for sale, and various self-made toys are also praised by all walks of life. Local people cannot help but call it convenient, etc., etc.

The New World Hotel at the end of Nicheng Bridge announced that since the renovation of the company, the business has been booming. Now, in order to seek the comfort and convenience of tourists, special personnel have been added to the stations and ports to welcome them. All vehicles and luggage do not require tourists to work themselves, which shows the thoughtful and meticulous service of the company, and the low prices are especially important, etc.

Theater News 253

Social Film Company announced that the company has been preparing for five months and has now rented No. 26 Tao'erfeisi Road as an office. Two films will be started within days, both written by Li Tiantian, one is called "The Righteous Hero" and the other is called "The Flower of Society", directed by Cai Qianyun and Wu Beihuan respectively. The drama still lacks several female actors, and is currently looking for them, and has hired two photography technicians who have returned from Fusang to be responsible for the production, etc.

The World Grand Theater at the corner of Qingyun Road, Zhabei, announced that the theater will show the latest romantic woman produced by Mingxing Film Company from today. This film is Ms. Xuan Jinglin's first carefully crafted masterpiece on the screen. Her performance is close to the style of American Swansen. It is a pity that each film she has starred in has not fully shown her strengths. Now, this film not only has a realistic performance, but also has a very tortuous plot that does not fall into the ordinary. The film has a considerable position in the domestic films, especially as a work that opens up a new aspect of love films, etc.

Fudan Film Company announced that the company has always been meticulous in making films. No matter what film it is, it is always pursued to be perfect, so every film is completed, customers are competing to purchase, so the company can also thrive. Now, the internal expansion has been greatly expanded to recruit specialized talents, so that the films produced in the future can be more advanced. In addition, the Fudan Drama Club has been organized to rehearse various excellent plays, dance and songs, in preparation for performing on stage when it is released publicly. This matter has been handled by Mr. Yu Boyan to hire drama experts to be responsible for, and is in progress. It is expected that on the day of the public release of the fifth episode of "Burning Seven Star Tower", we will be able to meet with the guests, etc.

Wanguo Film Company announced that the company's first creative blockbuster "Terror Night" was produced by Chen Yixing and Yu Xia, co-directed by He Zhigang and Lu Hanping, written by Li Changjian, explained by Shen Xinfu, male lead Chen Yulou, Zhang Zhizhen, female lead Hua Wanfang, has now been filmed and will be tested in a few days. The second production, the martial arts mechanism blockbuster "Heroes", is currently rushing to make costumes and will go to Suzhou in a few days to take exterior shots. The company's new address is No. 111, intersection of Baoshan Road and Yokohama Road, Zhabei, etc.

Minghua Film Company announced that the company has made a surprise attack with the spirit of Wu Chang and the talents of the Hui Cui. After a difficult business, it has gathered the efforts and experience of many people to form a film giant structure. The film is named "Two Heroes of the East", depicting the evil society and being eliminated by the two swordsmen. There are many unique scenes in the drama, and the scenery is even more grand and magnificent. Film merchants who want to order or rent and show the film can visit our office at No. 1, Hongning Lane, Caishi Road, for contact, etc.

Jincheng Five Star Film Company announced that the company is now cooperating on both sides, purchasing a photography field and self-provided office. Exterior shots will be started within days, and two films will be started at the same time, one is "Lone Flying Hero" and the other is the fashion "Passionate Hero". The selected scripts also include "Night Exploration of Xiechun Tower", "Lihentian", "Green Forest Hero", "Falling Flowers and Flowing Water Spring Goes Away", "Hero Slaying Demon", "New Romance of Flowers and Moon" and other dramas, etc.
